To use ChatGPT AI, please ensure that the following requirements are met:
Visual Studio Code version 1.73.0 or later is installed on your system.
You have an OpenAI API key or ChatGPT access token.
Installation
To use this extension, install it from the VSCode marketplace.
--
After completing these steps, the extension should be ready to use.
API Modes
Currently, there are two modes for accessing the API: "ChatGPTAPI" and "ChatGPTUnofficialProxyAPI".
ChatGPTAPI
To use this extension, you will need an&nbsp;API key&nbsp;from OpenAI. To obtain one, follow these steps:
--
Copy the key and paste it into the&nbsp;API Key&nbsp;field in the extension settings.
ChatGPTUnofficialProxyAPI
To use the ChatGPTUnofficialProxyAPI, you need an OpenAI access token from the ChatGPT web app. You can
obtain the access token in either of two ways:
Use&nbsp;acheong08/OpenAIAuth, which is a Python script to automatically log in and get an access token. This
method works only with email and password accounts; it does not support accounts where you authenticate via

Microsoft or Google.
Manually get an access token by logging in to the ChatGPT web app and
opening&nbsp;https://chat.openai.com/api/auth/session, which will return a JSON object containing your access token
string.
Access tokens last for approximately eight hours.
Building from source (not applicable for VSCode marketplace version)
To build the extension from source, clone the repository and run&nbsp;npm install&nbsp;to install the dependencies.
--

easier. It allows users to define and train neural networks using a concise and intuitive syntax.&nbsp;
tflearn provides a wide range of built-in layers, optimizers, activation functions, and evaluation metrics.&nbsp;

Theano works by building a computational graph where mathematical operations are represented as nodes and their
dependencies as edges. This graph is then compiled into highly optimized C code, allowing it to be executed on
various hardware architectures.&nbsp;
--
Detectron2 becomes a flexible and efficient platform for developers to create computer vision models. It works by
leveraging a modular design and a powerful backbone network architecture.&nbsp;

because of its flexibility, powerful architecture, and extensive features.

to development tools, Unity can only create an Xcode project for an iOS game or app and not build the binary directly.

potential merges with the boundless possibilities of AI. We'll create a world that whispers echoes of Terminator and
Matrix, yet rooted in the vastness of our universe.
--
Matrix themes with real-world planetary environments.
But here's what I have accomplished:
Design and World Building:
I generated stunning concept art using NightCafe Creator and Artbreeder, capturing the essence of Terminator and
Matrix aesthetics.
I incorporated real-world satellite imagery and maps, creating breathtaking landscapes and planetary vistas.
I began designing the AI Agents, imbuing them with personality traits and emotional depth.
AI Integration and APIs:
I integrated Hugging Face Transformers for natural language processing, allowing AI Agents to understand and
respond to user queries.
I set up Bard to assist with creative writing and storytelling, enabling AI Agents to engage in personalized narratives.
I connected to Teachable Machine, allowing users to build their own AI-powered games and simulations within the
metaverse.
WordPress and Snowflake:
I used Figma 2 AI web cloner to build the basic WordPress website framework, incorporating generated concept art
and imagery.
I started writing Python code for the Snowflake backend, focusing on user account creation and avatar customization.
